<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неосвещенный.html>неосвещённый</a> (29898)</h1><br><hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:оса.html>о́с</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ве<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>щён<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вки</a>: <b>не-о-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-свещ-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ённ</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b>.
